--- Context from: /users/lee/workspaces/ai/live-bot/gemini.md ---
# Streamix (Live Bot) Project Context

This file provides foundational mandates and project context for AI agents working on the Streamix codebase. Streamix is a high-performance Bilibili live stream assistant built with Rust and Tauri.

## Project Overview

Streamix (formerly Live Bot) is an AI-powered assistant for Bilibili streamers. It provides real-time monitoring, automated interaction (welcomes, thanks, keyword replies), and advanced AI Agent capabilities.

### Core Architecture
- **Frontend**: React (TypeScript) + Vite, running within the Tauri shell. Located in `src-tauri/`.
- **Backend (Tauri Commands)**: Rust-based Tauri commands that interface with the bot logic. Located in `src/main.rs`.
- **Bot Logic**: Modular engine for processing live events. Located in `src/bot/`.
- **API Integration**: Bilibili-specific HTTP and WebSocket protocol implementations.
  - `src/api.rs`: Bilibili HTTP API (login, room info, etc.).
  - `crates/bilibili-live-protocol`: Custom crate for parsing Bilibili WebSocket events.
- **Voice Capabilities**: Specialized crate for ASR (Speech-to-Text) and TTS (Text-to-Speech). Located in `crates/voice/`.
- **Storage**: SQLite-based persistence for interaction records and sessions. Located in `src/storage/`.

## Building and Running

### Prerequisites
- Rust (Stable)
- Node.js (Latest LTS)
- pnpm (Recommended)

### Commands
- **Run Development Mode**: `cargo run --features tauri` (Starts both the Rust backend and Vite frontend).
- **Build Frontend**: `npm run build` inside `src-tauri/`.
- **Build Release Binary**: `cargo build --release --features tauri`.
- **Run Tests**: `cargo test --workspace`.
- **Linting**: `cargo fmt --check` and `npm run lint` inside `src-tauri/`.

## Development Conventions

### Backend (Rust)
- **Async/Await**: Heavy use of `tokio` for asynchronous task management.
- **Error Handling**: Use `anyhow` for flexible error propagation in application logic.
- **Feature Flags**: The `tauri` feature flag controls the inclusion of the desktop GUI components.
- **Event Handling**: Live events are processed through `BotEngine::handle_event`, which returns a vector of response strings.

### Frontend (React/TS)
- **Styling**: Tailwind CSS v4 with specialized "Liquid Glass" glassmorphism effects.
- **State Management**: React state and hooks, with Tauri `invoke` for backend communication.
- **UI Components**: Uses Radix UI primitives and Lucide icons.

### Data Management
- **Persistence**: SQLite is used for all long-term data.
- **Credentials**: Bilibili tokens and refresh tokens are stored in the `token/` directory.
- **Configuration**: Application configuration is stored in `etc/bilidanmaku-api.yaml`.

## Key Files & Directories
- `src/main.rs`: The heartbeat of the application, managing the Tauri lifecycle and command registration.
- `src/bot/engine.rs`: The central logic for filtering and responding to live events.
- `src/api.rs`: The gateway to Bilibili's web services.
- `crates/bilibili-live-protocol/src/lib.rs`: The parser for Bilibili's live binary protocol.
- `docs/roadmap.md`: The strategic plan for the project's evolution.
--- End of Context from: /users/lee/workspaces/ai/live-bot/gemini.md ---

## MODEL вЬ®

I have resolved the compilation errors and targeted warnings in the project.

### Summary of Changes:

1.  **Resolved Dependency Issues**:
    *   Added `tauri-plugin-opener` to `Cargo.toml` and enabled it in the `tauri` feature.
    *   Updated `src/main.rs` to initialize the `tauri-plugin-opener` plugin in the `tauri::Builder`.

2.  **Fixed Compilation Errors in `src/main.rs`**:
    *   **Unresolved Module**: Replaced the incorrect `tauri_plugin_opener::open` calls with the correct Tauri v2 API: `app.opener().open_url()` and `app.opener().open_path()`, using the `OpenerExt` trait.
    *   **Struct Initialization**: Removed the redundant `danmaku_buffer` field initialization from `SharedState` and `BufferedEmitter`, as they were either missing from the struct definition or never used.
    *   **Syntax Errors**: Cleaned up unexpected closing delimiters at the end of `src/main.rs` introduced during edits.

3.  **Fixed Warnings**:
    *   **Mutability**: Removed an unnecessary `mut` qualifier for the `vad` parameter in `crates/voice/src/sherpa_vad/mod.rs`.
    *   **Unused Fields**: Removed the unused `danmaku_buffer` field from the `BufferedEmitter` struct to resolve compiler warnings.

The workspace now compiles successfully with `cargo check --workspace --all-targets --features tauri`. Remaining warnings are related to unused code in the wider project, which are typical for the current state of development.

## MODEL вЬ®

**Implementing Mouse-Driven Dynamics** I'm currently exploring how to tie the background gradient's perceived depth and position to the user's mouse movements. My immediate focus is on integrating this interactive element with the existing animated blobs in `BackgroundBlobs.tsx`, potentially by adjusting CSS variables defined in `theme.css`.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "update_topic",
  "args": {
    "strategic_intent": "Implementing an interactive mouse-following background effect.",
    "title": "Adding Interactive Background Depth",
    "summary": "The user wants the background depth to follow mouse movement. I'm updating `BackgroundBlobs.tsx` to include an interactive spotlight effect. I'll add mouse movement tracking using React state and apply a smooth transform to a new spotlight blob. This will create a subtle but noticeable \"depth\" effect that reacts to user interaction, further enhancing the \"Liquid Glass\" aesthetic. I'll ensure the effect is performant by using `translate3d` and maintaining appropriate opacity levels."
  },
  "id": "update_topic_1778551065208_0"
}
```**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "replace",
  "args": {

### ж†ЄењГжФєињЫпЉЪ

I'm prioritizing fixing this type mismatch.**Resolving Danmu Inconsistencies** I've pinpointed the core issue: `api.getRecentDanmaku()` drains the shared danmaku buffer. 'зЫСеРђдЄ≠пЉМз≠ЙеЊЕеЉєеєХ...' : 'зВєеЗїеП≥дЄЛиІТ вЦґ еЉАеІЛиОЈеПЦ'}\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n      </GlassCard>\n\n      <GlassCard className=\"p-4\">\n        <div className=\"flex gap-2\">\n          <Input\n            value={message}\n            onChange={(e) => setMessage(e.target.value)}\n            onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && sendDanmu()}\n            placeholder=\"иЊУеЕ•и¶БеПСйАБзЪДеЉєеєХпЉИжЬАе§Ъ 30 е≠ЧпЉЙвА¶\"\n            className=\"flex-1\"\n            maxLength={30}\n          />\n          <Button variant=\"primary\" onClick={sendDanmu} disabled={!message.trim()}>\n            еПСйАБ\n          </Button>\n          {!isMonitoring && (\n            <button\n              onClick={toggleMonitor}\n              title=\"еЉАеІЛиОЈеПЦ\"\n              className=\"w-9 h-9 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/10 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/20 hover:bg-white/80 transition-all flex-shrink-0\"\n            >\n              <Play className=\"w-4 h-4\" />\n            </button>\n          )}\n          <button\n            onClick={checkMonitorStatus}\n            title=\"еИЈжЦ∞зКґжАБ\"\n            className=\"w-9 h-9 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/10 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/20 hover:bg-white/80 transition-all flex-shrink-0\"\n          >\n            <RefreshCw className=\"w-4 h-4\" />\n          </button>\n        </div>\n        <div className=\"text-[10px] text-gray-400 mt-2 text-right\">\n          {message.length}/30\n        </div>\n      </GlassCard>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}

## MODEL вЬ®

**Investigating log output** I'm currently tracking down why the specific "жµЛиѓХеЉєеєХ" log isn't appearing in the backend console, though I am successfully capturing other "еЉєеєХ" events like `[Monitor] Event: еЉєеєХ иРљжЧ•жЄЄж∞С: дљ†е•љеХК` in my `monitor.rs` changes.**Analyzing frontend requests** I've confirmed the backend is correctly buffering and emitting test messages. The issue seems to stem from the frontend's interaction, as `get_recent_danmaku` isn't returning anything, or the frontend isn't processing the data it receives. I'm now focusing on frontend console logs.**Verifying Backend Buffering** I've confirmed the backend logic for capturing and buffering danmaku messages is executing correctly. The logs now clearly show the `[Monitor] Captured Danmu` events, indicating the `danmaku_buffer` is being populated. My focus is shifting back to the `get_recent_danmaku` function in `main.rs` to understand its interaction with the buffer.**Debugging frontend parsing** I've identified that the backend correctly captures and buffers danmaku events. The crucial detail is that the `line` being pushed to the buffer is the `event.to_string()` output, which differs from what the frontend expects. I'm now examining `Monitor.tsx` to understand how it parses these logs.**Tracing log transmission** I've confirmed the backend correctly formats danmaku logs as "еЉєеєХ User: Content," which matches the frontend parser's expectations. My current focus is on ensuring the `get_recent_danmaku` function in the frontend is being called and is successfully retrieving data from the API.**Tool Command**:
```json

  "name": "update_topic",
  "args": {

## MODEL вЬ®

**Reviewing Monitor.tsx Code** I'm currently analyzing the `Monitor.tsx` code. My focus is on identifying potential issues, specifically noting that the `setup` function is asynchronous without being awaited. I've also observed that timer management (`pollTimer`, `flushTimer`) within `useEffect` appears to be handled correctly.**Investigating Danmaku Flow** I've pinpointed a crucial detail: `parseMonitorLog` filters out nulls, and the ID increment logic seems sound. The real breakthrough came when I noticed backend logs confirming `danmaku_buf_cb` is indeed updated, despite frontend reports of empty arrays. I suspect a discrepancy in `MonitorHandle` usage.**Clarifying Buffer Handling** I'm digging into how the `danmaku_buf` is being managed. It appears `run_monitor_loop` receives a clone, which is then moved into `ws_task` and further cloned to create `danmaku_buf_cb`. This `danmaku_buf_cb` is then passed to `run_parsed_client`, suggesting a shared `Arc<Mutex<Vec<String>>>` is in play.**Refining Polling Logic** I've identified a potential race condition. It seems `getRecentDanmaku` might be called too frequently, draining the buffer before the UI can update. While `bufferRef.current.push(entry)` handles frontend buffering, the interaction with `flushLogs` needs closer examination to ensure no danmaku is lost between polling cycles.**Identifying Buffer Loss** I've discovered the root of the problem: I mistakenly removed `danmaku_buffer` from `SharedState` initialization. This omission means the buffer isn't being properly managed, leading to data loss. The fix involves re-adding it to `SharedState`.**Correcting Local Buffer Scope** I've realized my mistake: a local `danmaku_buf` was being created and stored within `MonitorHandle` in `start_monitor`. This prevents `get_recent_danmaku` from accessing the correct buffer, as it only locks the local, and thus empty, buffer. The fix is to use the shared `monitor_log_buffer` from `SharedState` for the `danmaku_buffer` field in `MonitorHandle`.**Finding State Reset Cause** I've discovered the issue: the `state.monitor` is being reset to `None` in `main.rs` by another part of the code that isn't directly related to the monitor's lifecycle. This premature clearing is what's causing the buffer to appear empty.**Detecting Timer Recreation** I'm now focusing on how `useEffect` in `Monitor.tsx` handles timer recreation. It appears a new polling timer is spawned on navigation, but the cleanup function isn't effectively preventing duplicates, potentially leading to a race condition between new and old timers.**Analyzing Danmaku Fetching** I'm examining the two distinct methods for fetching danmaku: polling and event listeners. The user reports seeing no danmaku, which suggests neither method is successfully populating the `bufferRef.current`. My next step is to verify if these buffers are actually being flushed to the `logs` state.**Confirming Buffer Drain** I've confirmed that `get_recent_danmaku` in `main.rs` correctly locks and drains the danmaku buffer. If no lines are appearing, it strongly suggests `state.monitor` might be `None`, or the "Start Monitor" button hasn't been pressed, even though the user indicates active monitoring.**Investigating Live Event Delivery** I'm scrutinizing how live events are being handled. The backend seems to be emitting them correctly, and the frontend logic for identifying danmaku messages (`event.type === 'Danmu'`) appears sound. My current focus is on the `onLiveEvent` listener itself to understand why these events aren't consistently reaching the UI.**Fixing Buffer Merging** I've identified that the "TEST" danmaku is correctly written to the buffer but not emitted as a live event. It is, however, appearing in `monitor-log`. This suggests a buffer polling or parsing failure, as the UI isn't updating. I'm now addressing the buffer merging issue in `Monitor.tsx` and adding more tracing.

**Addressing Scroll Issues**

I'm investigating the `overflow-hidden` and `overflow-y-auto` CSS properties applied to the main container and inner div within the `Monitor` component. This styling might be inadvertently hiding the danmaku messages, even if they are being correctly rendered, causing the user to perceive them as missing.**Tool Command**:
```json
{

### 1. иЃЊзљЃйЭҐжЭњ UI жЈ±еЇ¶дЉШеМЦ
йТИеѓєвАЬйҐЬиЙ≤дЄНеМЇеИЖгАБжЦЗе≠ЧдЄНжШОжШЊвАЭзЪДйЧЃйҐШпЉМжИСињЫи°МдЇЖдї•дЄЛжФєињЫпЉЪ

text.startsWith('зЇҐеМЕ ') || text.startsWith('е§©йАЙ ')) {\n    return { id, type: 'other', text, time };\n  }\n  // Skip high-frequency popularity heartbeats\n  if (text.startsWith('дЇЇж∞Ф ')) return null;\n  // All other messages (system/connection/status)\n  return { id, type: 'system', text, time };\n}\n\nconst typeColors: Record<LogType, string> = {\n  danmu: 'text-sky-600 dark:text-sky-400',\n  gift: 'text-amber-600 dark:text-amber-400',\n  interact: 'text-green-600 dark:text-green-400',\n  other: 'text-purple-600 dark:text-purple-400',\n  system: 'text-gray-400',\n};\n\nconst typeBadge: Record<LogType, string> = {\n  danmu: 'еЉєеєХ',\n  gift: 'з§ЉзЙ©',\n  interact: 'дЇТеК®',\n  other: 'еЕґдїЦ',\n  system: 'з≥їзїЯ',\n};\n\nexport function Monitor() {\n  const [filter, setFilter] = useState('all');\n  const [message, setMessage] = useState('');\n  const [isMonitoring, setIsMonitoring] = useState(false);\n  const [logs, setLogs] = useState<LogEntry[]>([]);\n  const logEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\n  const bufferRef = useRef<LogEntry[]>([]);\n  const loggedIn = useLoggedIn();\n\n  // Flush buffered log entries every 200ms for smooth real-time display\n  const flushLogs = useCallback(() => {\n    if (bufferRef.current.length === 0) return;\n    const itemsToFlush = [...bufferRef.current];\n    bufferRef.current = [];\n    setLogs(prev => {\n      const next = [...prev, ...itemsToFlush];\n      return next.length > 500 ? next.slice(next.length - 500) : next;\n    });\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    checkMonitorStatus();\n    \n    // Load buffered history immediately so page shows logs on first open\n    api.getMonitorLogs().then(rawLogs => {\n      const history = rawLogs\n        .map(parseMonitorLog)\n        .filter((e): e is LogEntry => e !== null)\n        .slice(-200);\n      \n      // Merge history with whatever is already in the buffer\n      bufferRef.current = [...history, ...bufferRef.current];\n      flushLogs();\n    }).catch(console.error);\n\n    // Poll danmaku buffer every 150ms (direct mpsc channel, no Tauri broadcast overhead)\n    const pollTimer = setInterval(async () => {\n      try {\n        const lines = await api.getRecentDanmaku();\n        if (lines.length > 0) {\n          for (const line of lines) {\n            const entry = parseMonitorLog(line);\n            if (entry) bufferRef.current.push(entry);\n          }\n        }\n      } catch (err) {\n        console.error('[Monitor] Polling error:', err);\n      }\n    }, 150);\n\n    // Batch flush to React state every 200ms\n    const flushTimer = setInterval(() => {\n      if (bufferRef.current.length > 0) {\n        flushLogs();\n      }\n    }, 200);\n\n    let unlistenLog: (() => void) | undefined;\n    let unlistenLive: (() => void) | undefined;\n    let unlistenStatus: (() => void) | undefined;\n\n    const setup = async () => {\n      unlistenLog = await api.onMonitorLog((text) => {\n        const entry = parseMonitorLog(text);\n        if (entry) bufferRef.current.push(entry);\n      });\n      unlistenLive = await api.onLiveEvent((parsed: any) => {\n        const event = parsed?.event ?? parsed;\n        const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();\n        const type = event?.type || event?.cmd;\n        if (type === 'Danmu' || type === 'DANMU_MSG') {\n          const user = event.user || event.info?.[2]?.[1] || 'жЬ™зЯ•';\n          const text = event.text || event.info?.[1] || '';\n          if (text) {\n            bufferRef.current.push({ id: _logId++, type: 'danmu', text: `еЉєеєХ ${user}: ${text}`, user, content: text, time });\n          }\n        }\n      });\n      unlistenStatus = await api.onMonitorStatus((status) => {\n        if (status === 'еЈ≤еБЬж≠Ґ') { setIsMonitoring(false); }\n        else if (status === 'ињРи°МдЄ≠') { setIsMonitoring(true); }\n      });\n    };\n    setup();\n\n    return () => {\n      clearInterval(pollTimer);\n      clearInterval(flushTimer);\n      if (unlistenLog) unlistenLog();\n      if (unlistenLive) unlistenLive();\n      if (unlistenStatus) unlistenStatus();\n    };\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    logEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });\n  }, [logs]);\n\n  const checkMonitorStatus = async () => {\n    try {\n      const status = await api.getMonitorStatus();\n      setIsMonitoring(status);\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to check monitor status:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const toggleMonitor = async () => {\n    if (!loggedIn) { toast.info('иѓЈеЕИзЩїељХ'); return; }\n    try {\n      if (isMonitoring) {\n        await api.stopMonitor();\n        setIsMonitoring(false);\n      } else {\n        await api.startMonitor();\n        setIsMonitoring(true);\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error(`жУНдљЬе§±иі•: ${err}`);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const sendDanmu = async () => {\n    if (!loggedIn) { toast.info('иѓЈеЕИзЩїељХ'); return; }\n    if (!message.trim()) return;\n    try {\n      await api.sendDanmu(message);\n      setMessage('');\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error(`еПСйАБе§±иі•: ${err}`);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const filters = [\n    { id: 'all', label: 'еЕ®йГ®' },\n    { id: 'danmaku', label: 'еЉєеєХ' },\n    { id: 'gift', label: 'з§ЉзЙ©' },\n    { id: 'interact', label: 'дЇТеК®' },\n    { id: 'other', label: 'еЕґдїЦ' },\n  ];\n\n  const filteredLogs = logs.filter(log => {\n    if (filter === 'all') return true;\n    if (filter === 'danmaku') return log.type === 'danmu';\n    if (filter === 'gift') return log.type === 'gift';\n    if (filter === 'interact') return log.type === 'interact';\n    if (filter === 'other') return log.type === 'other' || log.type === 'system';\n    return true;\n  });\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"p-4 h-full flex flex-col gap-4 overflow-hidden\">\n      <GlassCard className=\"flex-1 p-4 flex flex-col overflow-hidden\">\n        <div className=\"flex items-center justify-between mb-3\">\n          <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1.5\">\n            <div className={`w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full ${isMonitoring ? 'bg-green-500 animate-pulse' : 'bg-gray-400'}`} />\n            <span className=\"text-[11px] text-gray-500\">{isMonitoring ? 'зЫСеРђдЄ≠' : 'жЬ™зЫСеРђ'}</span>\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"flex gap-1.5\">\n            {filters.map((f) => (\n              <button\n                key={f.id}\n                onClick={() => setFilter(f.id)}\n                className={`px-3 py-1 rounded-lg text-[11px] transition-all ${\n                  filter === f.id\n                    ? 'bg-[var(--primary-color)] text-white'\n                    : 'bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/10 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/20 hover:bg-white/80'\n                }`}\n              >\n                {f.label}\n              </button>\n            ))}\n            <button\n              onClick={() => setLogs([])}\n              className=\"px-3 py-1 rounded-lg text-[11px] bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/10 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/20 hover:bg-white/80\"\n            >\n              жЄЕз©Ї\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"flex-1 overflow-y-auto space-y-0.5 bg-black/5 dark:bg-black/20 p-3 rounded-lg\">\n          {filteredLogs.map((log) => (\n            <div\n              key={log.id}\n              className=\"flex items-start gap-2 py-1 border-b border-black/5 dark:border-white/5 text-[11px]\"\n            >\n              <span className=\"text-gray-400 shrink-0 font-mono w-[52px]\">{log.time}</span>\n              <span className={`shrink-0 font-semibold w-[28px] ${typeColors[log.type]}`}>\n                {typeBadge[log.type]}\n              </span>\n              <span className=\"break-all\">\n                {log.type === 'danmu' ? (\n                  <>\n                    <span className=\"font-medium\">{log.user}</span>\n                    <span className=\"text-gray-400 mx-1\">:</span>\n                    <span>{log.content}</span>\n                  </>\n                ) : (\n                  <span className={log.type === 'system' ? 'text-gray-400 italic' : ''}>{log.text}</span>\n                )}\n              </span>\n            </div>\n          ))}\n          <div ref={logEndRef} />\n          {filteredLogs.length === 0 && (\n            <div className=\"text-gray-400 text-center py-10 italic text-[11px]\">\n              {isMonitoring ? 'зЫСеРђдЄ≠пЉМз≠ЙеЊЕеЉєеєХ...' : 'зВєеЗїеП≥дЄЛиІТ вЦґ еЉАеІЛиОЈеПЦ'}\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n      </GlassCard>\n\n      <GlassCard className=\"p-4\">\n        <div className=\"flex gap-2\">\n          <Input\n            value={message}\n            onChange={(e) => setMessage(e.target.value)}\n            onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && sendDanmu()}\n            placeholder=\"иЊУеЕ•и¶БеПСйАБзЪДеЉєеєХпЉИжЬАе§Ъ 30 е≠ЧпЉЙвА¶\"\n            className=\"flex-1\"\n            maxLength={30}\n          />\n          <Button variant=\"primary\" onClick={sendDanmu} disabled={!message.trim()}>\n            еПСйАБ\n          </Button>\n          {!isMonitoring && (\n            <button\n              onClick={toggleMonitor}\n              title=\"еЉАеІЛиОЈеПЦ\"\n              className=\"w-9 h-9 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/10 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/20 hover:bg-white/80 transition-all flex-shrink-0\"\n            >\n              <Play className=\"w-4 h-4\" />\n            </button>\n          )}\n          <button\n            onClick={checkMonitorStatus}\n            title=\"еИЈжЦ∞зКґжАБ\"\n            className=\"w-9 h-9 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/10 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/20 hover:bg-white/80 transition-all flex-shrink-0\"\n          >\n            <RefreshCw className=\"w-4 h-4\" />\n          </button>\n        </div>\n        <div className=\"text-[10px] text-gray-400 mt-2 text-right\">\n          {message.length}/30\n        </div>\n      </GlassCard>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"

content?: string;\n  time: string;\n}\n\nlet _logId = 0;\n\nfunction parseMonitorLog(text: string): LogEntry | null {\n  if (!text) return null;\n  const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();\n  const id = _logId++;\n\n  if (text.startsWith('еЉєеєХ ')) {\n    const rest = text.slice(3);\n    const colonIdx = rest.indexOf(': ');\n    if (colonIdx >= 0) {\n      return { id, type: 'danmu', text, user: rest.slice(0, colonIdx), content: rest.slice(colonIdx + 2), time };\n    }\n    return { id, type: 'danmu', text, time };\n  }\n  if (text.startsWith('з§ЉзЙ© ') || text.startsWith('е§ІиИ™жµЈ ')) {\n    return { id, type: 'gift', text, time };\n  }\n  if (\n    text.startsWith('ињЫеЬЇ ') || text.startsWith('ињЫеЬЇзЙєжХИ ') ||\n    text.startsWith('еЕ≥ж≥® ') || text.startsWith('еИЖдЇЂ ') || text.startsWith('дЇТеК® ')\n  ) {\n    return { id, type: 'interact', text, time };\n  }\n  if (text.startsWith('з¶Би®А ') || text.startsWith('PK ') || text.startsWith('зЇҐеМЕ ') || text.startsWith('е§©йАЙ ')) {\n    return { id, type: 'other', text, time };\n  }\n  // Skip high-frequency popularity heartbeats\n  if (text.startsWith('дЇЇж∞Ф ')) return null;\n  // All other messages (system/connection/status)\n  return { id, type: 'system', text, time };\n}\n\nconst typeColors: Record<LogType, string> = {\n  danmu: 'text-sky-600 dark:text-sky-400',\n  gift: 'text-amber-600 dark:text-amber-400',\n  interact: 'text-green-600 dark:text-green-400',\n  other: 'text-purple-600 dark:text-purple-400',\n  system: 'text-gray-400',\n};\n\nconst typeBadge: Record<LogType, string> = {\n  danmu: 'еЉєеєХ',\n  gift: 'з§ЉзЙ©',\n  interact: 'дЇТеК®',\n  other: 'еЕґдїЦ',\n  system: 'з≥їзїЯ',\n};\n\nexport function Monitor() {\n  const [filter, setFilter] = useState('all');\n  const [message, setMessage] = useState('');\n  const [isMonitoring, setIsMonitoring] = useState(false);\n  const [logs, setLogs] = useState<LogEntry[]>([]);\n  const logEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\n  const bufferRef = useRef<LogEntry[]>([]);\n  const loggedIn = useLoggedIn();\n\n  // Flush buffered log entries every 200ms for smooth real-time display\n  const flushLogs = useCallback(() => {\n    if (bufferRef.current.length === 0) return;\n    const itemsToFlush = [...bufferRef.current];\n    bufferRef.current = [];\n    setLogs(prev => {\n      const next = [...prev, ...itemsToFlush];\n      return next.length > 500 ? next.slice(next.length - 500) : next;\n    });\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    checkMonitorStatus();\n    \n    // Load buffered history immediately so page shows logs on first open\n    api.getMonitorLogs().then(rawLogs => {\n      const history = rawLogs\n        .map(parseMonitorLog)\n        .filter((e): e is LogEntry => e !== null)\n        .slice(-200);\n      \n      // Merge history with whatever is already in the buffer\n      bufferRef.current = [...history, ...bufferRef.current];\n      flushLogs();\n    }).catch(console.error);\n\n    // Poll danmaku buffer every 150ms (direct mpsc channel, no Tauri broadcast overhead)\n    const pollTimer = setInterval(async () => {\n      try {\n        const lines = await api.getRecentDanmaku();\n        if (lines.length > 0) {\n          for (const line of lines) {\n            const entry = parseMonitorLog(line);\n            if (entry) bufferRef.current.push(entry);\n          }\n        }\n      } catch (err) {\n        console.error('[Monitor] Polling error:', err);\n      }\n    }, 150);\n\n    // Batch flush to React state every 200ms\n    const flushTimer = setInterval(() => {\n      if (bufferRef.current.length > 0) {\n        flushLogs();\n      }\n    }, 200);\n\n    let unlistenLog: (() => void) | undefined;\n    let unlistenLive: (() => void) | undefined;\n    let unlistenStatus: (() => void) | undefined;\n\n    const setup = async () => {\n      unlistenLog = await api.onMonitorLog((text) => {\n        const entry = parseMonitorLog(text);\n        if (entry) bufferRef.current.push(entry);\n      });\n      unlistenLive = await api.onLiveEvent((parsed: any) => {\n        const event = parsed?.event ?? parsed;\n        const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();\n        const type = event?.type || event?.cmd;\n        if (type === 'Danmu' || type === 'DANMU_MSG') {\n          const user = event.user || event.info?.[2]?.[1] || 'жЬ™зЯ•';\n          const text = event.text || event.info?.[1] || '';\n          if (text) {\n            bufferRef.current.push({ id: _logId++, type: 'danmu', text: `еЉєеєХ ${user}: ${text}`, user, content: text, time });\n          }\n        }\n      });\n      unlistenStatus = await api.onMonitorStatus((status) => {\n        if (status === 'еЈ≤еБЬж≠Ґ') { setIsMonitoring(false); }\n        else if (status === 'ињРи°МдЄ≠') { setIsMonitoring(true); }\n      });\n    };\n    setup();\n\n    return () => {\n      clearInterval(pollTimer);\n      clearInterval(flushTimer);\n      if (unlistenLog) unlistenLog();\n      if (unlistenLive) unlistenLive();\n      if (unlistenStatus) unlistenStatus();\n    };\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    logEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });\n  }, [logs]);\n\n  const checkMonitorStatus = async () => {\n    try {\n      const status = await api.getMonitorStatus();\n      setIsMonitoring(status);\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to check monitor status:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const toggleMonitor = async () => {\n    if (!loggedIn) { toast.info('иѓЈеЕИзЩїељХ'); return; }\n    try {\n      if (isMonitoring) {\n        await api.stopMonitor();\n        setIsMonitoring(false);\n      } else {\n        await api.startMonitor();\n        setIsMonitoring(true);\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error(`жУНдљЬе§±иі•: ${err}`);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const sendDanmu = async () => {\n    if (!loggedIn) { toast.info('иѓЈеЕИзЩїељХ'); return; }\n    if (!message.trim()) return;\n    try {\n      await api.sendDanmu(message);\n      setMessage('');\n    } catch (err) {\n      toast.error(`еПСйАБе§±иі•: ${err}`);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const filters = [\n    { id: 'all', label: 'еЕ®йГ®' },\n    { id: 'danmaku', label: 'еЉєеєХ' },\n    { id: 'gift', label: 'з§ЉзЙ©' },\n    { id: 'interact', label: 'дЇТеК®' },\n    { id: 'other', label: 'еЕґдїЦ' },\n  ];\n\n  const filteredLogs = logs.filter(log => {\n    // Completely exclude system logs from the interactive feed\n    if (log.type === 'system') return false;\n    \n    if (filter === 'all') return true;\n    if (filter === 'danmaku') return log.type === 'danmu';\n    if (filter === 'gift') return log.type === 'gift';\n    if (filter === 'interact') return log.type === 'interact';\n    if (filter === 'other') return log.type === 'other';\n    return true;\n  });\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"p-4 h-full flex flex-col gap-4 overflow-hidden\">\n      <GlassCard className=\"flex-1 p-4 flex flex-col overflow-hidden\">\n        <div className=\"flex items-center justify-between mb-3\">\n          <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n            <div className={`w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full ${isMonitoring ? 'bg-green-500 animate-pulse' : 'bg-gray-400'}`} />\n            <span className=\"text-[11px] font-medium text-gray-500\">\n              {isMonitoring ? 'ињЮжО•жИРеКЯпЉМж≠£еЬ®еРМж≠•иЃ∞ељХ...' : 'жЬ™зЫСеРђ'}\n            </span>\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"flex gap-1.5\">\n            {filters.map((f) => (\n              <button\n                key={f.id}\n                onClick={() => setFilter(f.id)}\n                className={`px-3 py-1 rounded-lg text-[11px] transition-all ${\n                  filter === f.id\n                    ? 'bg-[var(--primary-color)] text-white'\n                    : 'bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/10 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/20 hover:bg-white/80'\n                }`}\n              >\n                {f.label}\n              </button>\n            ))}\n            <button\n              onClick={() => setLogs([])}\n              className=\"px-3 py-1 rounded-lg text-[11px] bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/10 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/20 hover:bg-white/80\"\n            >\n              жЄЕз©ЇиЃ∞ељХ\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"flex-1 overflow-y-auto space-y-0.5 bg-black/5 dark:bg-black/20 p-3 rounded-lg\">\n          {filteredLogs.map((log) => (\n            <div\n              key={log.id}\n              className=\"flex items-start gap-2 py-1 border-b border-black/5 dark:border-white/5 text-[11px]\"\n            >\n              <span className=\"text-gray-400 shrink-0 font-mono w-[52px]\">{log.time}</span>\n              <span className={`shrink-0 font-semibold w-[28px] ${typeColors[log.type]}`}>\n                {typeBadge[log.type]}\n              </span>\n              <span className=\"break-all\">\n                {log.type === 'danmu' ? (\n                  <>\n                    <span className=\"font-medium\">{log.user}</span>\n                    <span className=\"text-gray-400 mx-1\">:</span>\n                    <span>{log.content}</span>\n                  </>\n                ) : (\n                  <span className={log.type === 'system' ? 'text-gray-400 italic' : ''}>{log.text}</span>\n                )}\n              </span>\n            </div>\n          ))}\n          <div ref={logEndRef} />\n          {filteredLogs.length === 0 && (\n            <div className=\"text-gray-400 text-center py-10 italic text-[11px]\">\n              {isMonitoring ? 'зЫСжОІдЄ≠пЉМз≠ЙеЊЕиЃ∞ељХ...' : 'зВєеЗїеП≥дЄЛиІТ вЦґ еЉАеІЛзЫСжОІ'}\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n      </GlassCard>\n\n      <GlassCard className=\"p-4\">\n        <div className=\"flex gap-2\">\n          <Input\n            value={message}\n            onChange={(e) => setMessage(e.target.value)}\n            onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && sendDanmu()}\n            placeholder=\"иЊУеЕ•и¶БеПСйАБзЪДеЉєеєХпЉИжЬАе§Ъ 30 е≠ЧпЉЙвА¶\"\n            className=\"flex-1\"\n            maxLength={30}\n          />\n          <Button \n            variant=\"primary\" \n            onClick={sendDanmu} \n            disabled={!loggedIn || !message.trim()}\n            className=\"min-w-[80px]\"\n          >\n            {!loggedIn ? 'иѓЈеЕИзЩїељХ' : !message.trim() ? 'иѓЈиЊУеЕ•еЖЕеЃє' : 'еПСйАБеЉєеєХ'}\n          </Button>\n          {!isMonitoring && (\n            <button\n              onClick={toggleMonitor}\n              title=\"еЉАеІЛзЫСжОІ\"\n              className=\"w-9 h-9 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/10 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/20 hover:bg-white/80 transition-all flex-shrink-0\"\n            >\n              <Play className=\"w-4 h-4\" />\n            </button>\n          )}\n          <button\n            onClick={checkMonitorStatus}\n            title=\"еИЈжЦ∞зКґжАБ\"\n            className=\"w-9 h-9 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/10 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/20 hover:bg-white/80 transition-all flex-shrink-0\"\n          >\n            <RefreshCw className=\"w-4 h-4\" />\n          </button>\n        </div>\n        <div className=\"text-[10px] text-gray-400 mt-2 text-right\">\n          {message.length}/30\n        </div>\n      </GlassCard>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```

  }

     toast.error(`жУНдљЬе§±иі•: ${err}`);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const sendDanmu = async () => {\n    if (!loggedIn) { toast.info('иѓЈеЕИзЩїељХ'); return; }\n    if (!message.trim()) return;\n    try {\n        try {\n          const room = await api.checkRoom(savedRoomId);\n          setAutoRoom({ roomId: String(room.room_id), liveStatus: room.live_status, liveTime: room.live_time ?? });\n    return () => unlisten?.();\n  }, [refreshUserInfo]);\n\n  const fetchLoginQr = async () => {\n    setLoadingQr(true);\n    setLoginStatus('pending');\n    try {\n      const data = await api.startLogin();\n      setLoginUrl(data.url);\n      setLoginKey(data.qrcode_key);\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('иОЈеПЦдЇМзїіз†Бе§±иі•:', err);\n    } finally {\n      setLoadingQr(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  // иљЃиѓҐзЩїељХзКґжАБ\n  useEffect(() => {\n    let timer: NodeJS.Timeout;\n    if (showLoginModal && loginKey && loginStatus !== 'success' && loginStatus !== 'expired') {\n      timer = setInterval(async () => {\n        try {\n          const res = await invoke<any>('poll_login', { key: loginKey });\n          if (res.status === 'Success') {\n            setLoginStatus('success');\n            setShowLoginModal(false);\n            setLoginUrl('');\n            setLoginKey('');\n            if (res.uid) {\n              setUserInfo({\n                uid: res.uid, uname: res.uname, face: res.face,\n                level: res.level ?? 0, vip_status: res.vip_status ?? 0,\n                vip_type: res.vip_type ?? 0, coins: res.coins ?? 0,\n                vip_nickname_color: res.vip_nickname_color ?? '',\n                is_login: true, saved_at: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000)\n              });\n            }\n            setIsLoggedIn(true);\n            setHasConnectedRoom(false);\n          } else if (res.status === 'Expired') {\n            setLoginStatus('expired');\n          }\n        } catch (err) {\n          console.error('Poll login error:', err);\n        }\n      }, 2000);\n    }\n    return () => { if (timer) clearInterval(timer); };\n  }, [showLoginModal, loginKey, loginStatus]);\n\n  const openLoginModal = () => {\n    setShowLoginModal(true);\n    setLoginUrl('');\n    setLoginKey('');\n    setLoginStatus('pending');\n    fetchLoginQr();\n  };\n\n  // йААеЗЇзЩїељХ\n  const handleLogout = useCallback(async () => {\n    await api.logout().catch(() => {});\n    setIsLoggedIn(false);\n    setUserInfo(null);\n    setAutoRoom(null);\n    setHasConnectedRoom(false);\n    window.location.reload();\n  }, []);\n\n  // жЬ™ињЮжО•жЧґзВєеЗїдЇ§дЇТеЕГзі†пЉМеЉєеЗЇжПРз§Ї\n  const triggerConnectHint = useCallback(() => {\n    toast.success('иѓЈињЮжО•жИњйЧі');\n  }, []);\n\n  // ињЮжО•жИњйЧіжИРеКЯ\n  const handleRoomConnected = useCallback((roomId: string, liveStatus: number, liveTime: string, roomUid?: number) => {\n    const id = parseInt(roomId);\n    setAutoRoom({ roomId, liveStatus, liveTime });\n    setShowRoomModal(false);\n    setHasConnectedRoom(true);\n    // жМБдєЕеМЦеЈ≤ињЮжО•зЪДжИњйЧі\n    api.setConnectedRoom(id).catch(() => {});\n    // жЛЙеПЦдЄїжТ≠дњ°жБѓ\n    if (roomUid) {\n      api.getAnchorInfo(roomUid).then(setAnchorInfo).catch(() => {});\n    }\n    // иЗ™еК®еРѓеК® WebSocket зЫСеРђ\n    api.startMonitor(id).catch(() => {});\n  }, []);\n\n  // жЦ≠еЉАжИњйЧі\n  const handleDisconnect = useCallback(() => {\n    setHasConnectedRoom(false);\n    setAnchorInfo(null);\n    api.stopMonitor().catch(() => {});\n    api.setConnectedRoom(null).catch(() => {});\n  }, []);\n\n  if (!loginChecked) return null;\n\n  return (\n    <ThemeProvider>\n      <Toaster\n        position=\"top-center\"\n        richColors\n        duration={1500}\n        closeButton\n        offset={72}\n        toastOptions={{\n          style: { width: 'fit-content', maxWidth: 360, fontSize: 12, padding: '8px 12px', minHeight: 36 },\n        }}\n      />\n      <LoginContext.Provider value={isLoggedIn}>\n      <HashRouter>\n        <div \n    onRefreshUserInfo={refreshUserInfo}\n              showConnectHint={showConnectHint}\n            />\n            <main className=\"flex-1 overflow-y-auto relative\">\n              {/*        )}\n              {!isLoggedIn && (\n                <div className=\"absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center z-20 bg-[var(--background)]/80 backdrop-blur-sm\">\n     <div className=\"text-[12px] text-gray-400\">зЩїељХеРОеН≥еПѓдљњзФ®жЙАжЬЙеКЯиГљ</div>\n                    <Button variant=\"primary\" onClick={openLoginModal}>\n                      <LogIn className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5 mr-1.5\" />\n                      жЙЂз†БзЩїељХ\n                    </Button>\n                  </GlassCard>\n                </div>\n              )}\n '', info.uid);\n    } catch (err: any) {\n      toast.error(`ињЮжО•е§±иі•: ${err}`);\n    } finally {\n      setLoading(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleMyRoom = () => {\n    if (!userRoom) { toast.error('зФ®жИЈдњ°жБѓжЬ™еК†иљљ'); return; }\n    setRoomId(String(userRoom.room_id));\n    onSuccess(String(userRoom.room_id), userRoom.live_status, userRoom.live_time ?? '', userRoom.uid);\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <>\n      <h2 className=\"text-[15px] font-semibold mb-4\">ињЮжО•зЫіжТ≠йЧі</h2>\n      <div className=\"space-y-4\">\n        <div>\n          <label className=\"text-[11px] text-gray-500 mb-1.5 block\">жИњйЧіеПЈ</label>\n          <div className=\"flex gap-2\">\n            <input\n              value={roomId}\n              onChange={(e) => setRoomId(e.target.value)}\n              placeholder=\"иѓЈиЊУеЕ•зЫіжТ≠йЧіжИњйЧіеПЈ\"\n              className=\"flex-1 h-[34px] px-3 rounded-lg bg-white/60 dark:bg-white/10 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/20 text-[12px] focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[var(--primary-color)]/50\"\n              onKeyDown={(e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter') handleConnect(); }}\n              autoFocus\n            />\n            <button\n              onClick={handleMyRoom}\n              disabled={!userRoom}\n              className=\"h-[34px] px-3 rounded-lg bg-[var(--primary-color)]/10 border border-[var(--primary-color)]/30 text-[var(--primary-color)] text-[11px] font-medium flex items-center gap-1 hover:bg-[var(--primary-color)]/20 transition-colors disabled:opacity-50\"\n              title=\"ињЮжО•жИСзЪДзЫіжТ≠йЧі\"\n            >\n              <Home className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5\" />\n              жИСзЪДжИњйЧі\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n      <div className=\"mt-6\">\n        <Button variant=\"primary\" className=\"w-full\" onClick={handleConnect} disabled={loading || !roomId}>\n          {loading ? 'ињЮжО•дЄ≠...' : 'ињЮжО•'}\n        </Button>\n      </div>\n    </>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}

## MODEL вЬ®

**Adapting Toaster Appearance** I'm currently working on updating the global toast's visual style to align with the Liquid Glass UI. My focus is on repositioning it to be centrally aligned over the right operation panel, ensuring it avoids the sidebar's space.**Refining Toaster Placement** I'm continuing to refine the toast's positioning. My current approach involves calculating the offset based on the sidebar's width to ensure the toast is correctly centered over the main content area, avoiding any overlap with the sidebar itself.**Calculating Toaster Offset** I'm re-evaluating how to position the toast. My current thinking is to use CSS variables to dynamically adjust the left offset based on the sidebar's width, ensuring it's centered within the right panel regardless of the sidebar's collapsed state.**Styling Toaster Background** I'm now focusing on the visual appearance of the toast. My current thoughts involve incorporating a backdrop blur effect, a semi-transparent background, and refined borders to enhance the glass-like aesthetic.

**Implementing Glass Look**

I plan to apply a backdrop blur, semi-transparent background, and better borders to the toaster for a glass effect. I'll investigate `sonner`'s viewport styling options.

**Adjusting Toaster Positioning**

I'm considering how to best position the toaster. My current approach is to directly style the `[data-sonner-toaster]` element to achieve the desired centered placement over the right operation panel.**Clarifying Toaster Placement** I'm now contemplating the precise positioning of the toast within the right operation panel. isActive = location.pathname === item.path;\n\n          return (\n            <Link\n              key={item.path}\n              to={item.path}\n              onClick={handleNavClick}\n              className={cn(\n                'flex items-center gap-3 h-[44px] px-3 rounded-xl transition-all border border-transparent',\n                isActive\n                  ? 'bg-[var(--sidebar-accent)] border-[var(--sidebar-primary)] text-[var(--sidebar-accent-foreground)]'\n                  : 'text-[var(--sidebar-foreground)] hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/5'\n              )}\n            >\n              <Icon className=\"w-4 h-4\" />\n              <span className=\"text-[12px] font-medium flex-1\">{item.label}</span>\n              {item.wip && (\n                <span className=\"text-[9px] text-gray-400 dark:text-gray-500 font-normal\">еЊЕеЉАеПС</span>\n              )}\n            </Link>\n          );\n        })}\n      </nav>\n\n      <div className=\"pt-3 border-t border-white/10 flex gap-2 flex-shrink-0\">\n        <IconButton onClick={onToggleSettings}>\n          <SettingsIcon className=\"w-4 h-4\" />\n        </IconButton>\n        <IconButton onClick={onToggleThemePanel}>\n          {theme === 'dark' ? <Moon className=\"w-4 h-4\" /> : <Sun className=\"w-4 h-4\" />}\n        </IconButton>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```
